    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Giant's father married Nan's mother so they are not half siblings, just step.<br/><br/>Same applied to Grant and Rush. Not blood brothers but they have always a<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Giant's father married Nan's mother so they are not half siblings, just step.<br /><br />Same applied to Grant and Rush. Not blood brothers but they have always accepted each other as siblings. Grant never liked Nan when they were growing up.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer638035170" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6450824967798565856"><b>3 stars that should have been 4 stars!!!</b><br/><br/>While I really enjoyed this book and wanted to give it 4 stars, the fact is, Nan–at least for me–made that rating impossible. Lets face it, all the Nan drama was simply annoying and nothing more than foolishness and filler. Her character became a distraction from rather than an assets to the story. <br/><br/>That said, I LOVED Rush and Blaire and their romance in this book. I was so please to see the unique and endearing characters I fell in love with in the first b</span>
  <span id="freeText6450824967798565856" style="display:none"><b>3 stars that should have been 4 stars!!!</b><br /><br />While I really enjoyed this book and wanted to give it 4 stars, the fact is, Nan–at least for me–made that rating impossible. Lets face it, all the Nan drama was simply annoying and nothing more than foolishness and filler. Her character became a distraction from rather than an assets to the story. <br /><br />That said, I LOVED Rush and Blaire and their romance in this book. I was so please to see the unique and endearing characters I fell in love with in the first book–who I felt went missing in the second–back again in this story. I sure do love these two! <br /><br />Other than Nan, I loved getting a satisfying dose of my favorite cast of characters from previous books. I especially loved the author teasing us with Grant and Harlow's points of view, which sets the stage, I hope, for the next book. <br /><br />And as for Rush, I'd give him <b>10 shiny stars</b> for his swoon-worthy and romantic wedding gifts. Oh, boy, did he sweep me off my feet! <br /><br />All in all, I really enjoyed this story and its HEA ending. <br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6450824967798565856" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer535833245" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3028583016888650338"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/70eb4f56-a21d-4649-a0e6-9ccc2d8bae96_zps6a87d147.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409584i/802034.jpg' alt=' photo 70eb4f56-a21d-4649-a0e6-9ccc2d8bae96_zps6a87d147.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Abbi Glines is one of my favorite NA/YA authors. I love everything she writes! This book wasn’t perfect, there are some things that could have been a bit different that could have made it better, I can see where everyone wouldn’t love it. But I sure loved it! Another Rush book? Hell yeah! <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/05f87029-b5a6-453b-8cfb-c5a145d25a86_zpsb3d3c7d7.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409584i/802035._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 05f87029-b5a6-453b-8cfb-c5a145d25a86_zpsb3d3c7d7.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Rush is the hottest of the hottest, the swoonyest of the swoonyest. He’s not perfect, but damn... I just love him! He has proved over and over again just how great he is, and just how much he </span>
  <span id="freeText3028583016888650338" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/70eb4f56-a21d-4649-a0e6-9ccc2d8bae96_zps6a87d147.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409584i/802034.jpg" alt=" photo 70eb4f56-a21d-4649-a0e6-9ccc2d8bae96_zps6a87d147.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Abbi Glines is one of my favorite NA/YA authors. I love everything she writes! This book wasn’t perfect, there are some things that could have been a bit different that could have made it better, I can see where everyone wouldn’t love it. But I sure loved it! Another Rush book? Hell yeah! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/05f87029-b5a6-453b-8cfb-c5a145d25a86_zpsb3d3c7d7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409584i/802035._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 05f87029-b5a6-453b-8cfb-c5a145d25a86_zpsb3d3c7d7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Rush is the hottest of the hottest, the swoonyest of the swoonyest. He’s not perfect, but damn... I just love him! He has proved over and over again just how great he is, and just how much he loves Blaire. This book is no exception. But he is being pulled in multiple directions. <br><b>
  <blockquote>“I love you, Blaire. I’m so damn proud of the fact that you’re going to be the mother of my son. I want everyone to know. Never doubt that.”</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/01b5b725-c533-44c1-905c-c3c62b10613f_zps88ee94ec.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409584i/802036._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 01b5b725-c533-44c1-905c-c3c62b10613f_zps88ee94ec.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Blaire is happy. Every thing in her life is starting to ‘fit’. She is pregnant by the love of her life and engaged to be married. She has a few close friends, and she’s trying to mend her relationship with her father. Blaire hasn’t had an easy life, but things are good for her now. Rush and her baby are the most important things to her, and she means everything to Rush. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/cc47d7f8-389e-4e53-acfe-f0aa2e5f3dfc_zpsb1b98b30.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409584i/802037.jpg" alt=" photo cc47d7f8-389e-4e53-acfe-f0aa2e5f3dfc_zpsb1b98b30.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><b>Blaire came first. Always.</b><br><br>Then Rush’s father, rock &amp; roll legend, Dean shows up. I thought Dean was awesome. But the reason he’s there... not so great. Nan has invaded his home in LA. She is being completely unreasonable and driving them all crazy. Dean’s bandmate is her ‘father’ and he just can’t handle all her drama. So Rush and Blaire decide to go after Thanksgiving and see if they can help... <br>Deans words:<br><i>
  <b>“You’re sister is a crazy bitch. She’s fucking insane. We need your help.”</b>
</i> And I couldn’t agree more. Nan is one <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/Forevertoofar-Nan_zpsc992cdb3.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409584i/802038.png" alt=" photo Forevertoofar-Nan_zpsc992cdb3.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She is just all kinds of awful to Blaire. Trying to put a wedge between Blaire and Rush. And she almost does. Rush is trying hard, but its difficult to manage Nan’s crazy, and his fiancee. Something extreme happens, Blaire just can’t take the drama anymore, and that feeling of never coming first to Rush. So she takes off to FL to see her dad. Rush, being the man he is, follows her. Rush realizes he can’t make Nan a priority anymore (than God!) that Blaire has to be number one- always. He can’t let her down again. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/565ff7d8-f442-4fc1-84a9-724c675aeee6_zps89869f21.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409584i/802039._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 565ff7d8-f442-4fc1-84a9-724c675aeee6_zps89869f21.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>From there, the book is just all kinds of sweet and sexy. Rush is hot as hell! The scenes between he and Blaire, even with her being pregnant are really steamy!<br><i>I could spend hours tasting her and having her come all over my tongue. It never got old. It was more of an addiction.</i><br> And there were some pretty funny lines as well, this is one of my favorites...<br><i>“I really wish I could confirm to him that you do in face have a penis. A very big and pretty penis.” <br>“Please, just call it big. Don’t call it pretty. That hurts its feelings.”</i><br>And I’m not going to lie... I got a little emotional at times. This book had me in tears. <br><i>“You are going to be the best husband and father that the world has ever known. One day our son’s wife will be thankful that her husband will have had you for a role model. She’ll be lucky because of you. Because you will have raised our son to be the man you are. He’ll love her completely because he’ll know how.”</i><br>  But my favorite part of the book... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The Wedding <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/36acde05-c27d-402c-b24c-e829f9da7802_zps51635447.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409584i/802040.jpg" alt=" photo 36acde05-c27d-402c-b24c-e829f9da7802_zps51635447.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I am kind of sad that Rush and Blaire’s story has ended, but I’m sure we will see more of them in the spin off series... for now- <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/1d2029cb-72fb-49b7-98a6-c91c2c72bf27_zps9f89be44.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409584i/802041.jpg" alt=" photo 1d2029cb-72fb-49b7-98a6-c91c2c72bf27_zps9f89be44.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Okay- Even though Blaire and Rush’s story is over, I am so happy we are getting another Woods book and a few Grant books! I only have one thing to say about Grant’s book... Abbi better not even try to get me to like Nan. Not. Going. To. Happen! I am at the point with her that there is NOTHING she could do to make me like her. We got a little teaser with Grant and Harlow’s p.o.v’s and I am getting really freaking excited for their books. I just love this series! For all Rush &amp; Blaire lovers, I’m sure you will enjoy this one!! :D<br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_560447599" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/560447599" />
    <a title="Elizabeth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5099622-elizabeth"><img alt="Elizabeth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389981285p2/5099622.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/560447599?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elizabeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elizabeth" href="/user/show/5099622-elizabeth">Elizabeth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5099622-elizabeth?shelf=worst-books-ever">worst-books-ever</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer560447599" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16567794187149080015">Actual rating: 1.5 very generous stars<br/><br/>Why did I do this to myself? I knew going in it would be a problem and I plowed right on ahead and did it anyway.<br/><a href='http://s1287.photobucket.com/user/EDODonn/media/shotmyself_zps00c6ba70.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413291ra/813558.gif' alt=' photo shotmyself_zps00c6ba70.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I should have run away screaming when my friend lent this to me. I should have listened to that little voice inside my head telling me...<br/><a href='http://s1287.photobucket.com/user/EDODonn/media/runawayoctopusnopenopenope_zpsf0b5dbc5.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413291ra/813559.gif' alt=' photo runawayoctopusnopenopenope_zpsf0b5dbc5.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>Sadly, I did not. <br/><br/>To me this book was merely a money-making venture. Seriously, this series could have very easily been completed with an epilogue. It would have been nice actually if the author had done </span>
  <span id="freeText16567794187149080015" style="display:none">Actual rating: 1.5 very generous stars<br><br>Why did I do this to myself? I knew going in it would be a problem and I plowed right on ahead and did it anyway.<br><a href="http://s1287.photobucket.com/user/EDODonn/media/shotmyself_zps00c6ba70.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413291ra/813558.gif" alt=" photo shotmyself_zps00c6ba70.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I should have run away screaming when my friend lent this to me. I should have listened to that little voice inside my head telling me...<br><a href="http://s1287.photobucket.com/user/EDODonn/media/runawayoctopusnopenopenope_zpsf0b5dbc5.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413291ra/813559.gif" alt=" photo runawayoctopusnopenopenope_zpsf0b5dbc5.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Sadly, I did not. <br><br>To me this book was merely a money-making venture. Seriously, this series could have very easily been completed with an epilogue. It would have been nice actually if the author had done this, as many others do, and offered it to her fans for free. Except then Abbi Glines wouldn't have had the opportunity to hook you on her other books. Like those she's very obviously planned for Grant and Woods. See, here's the thing, a huge component of this novel is dedicated to other characters and setting up their own stories. Entire chapters are dedicated to completely irrelevant story arcs. Listen, if I find Grant or Woods so interesting I'll read their stories, I don't need or want you taking away from other characters to push your agenda.<br><a href="http://s1287.photobucket.com/user/EDODonn/media/bigbangtheorysheldonitsatrap_zps29a05970.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413291ra/813560.gif" alt=" photo bigbangtheorysheldonitsatrap_zps29a05970.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>To make matters worse, and to further solidify my point, the author had the balls to throw an advertisement into the middle of a chapter. Really, I shit you not. Right there in the wedding scene, she actually interrupts it to direct the reader to buy Rush Finlay's song on iTunes. What?<br><a href="http://s1287.photobucket.com/user/EDODonn/media/tumblr_ll39e709kG1qdoqnm_zps709a4e22.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413291ra/813561.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_ll39e709kG1qdoqnm_zps709a4e22.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is little in the way of actual plot in this installment. It's really just an excuse to watch Rush and Blaire play house and engage in the simple pleasantries of pre-marital bliss. I guess if you're into that, then go for it, 'cause that's what you're gonna get. Yes, there's drama when Nan busts back on the scene but honestly, I hate her so much at this point I wanted to skip those scenes entirely so they added nothing of consequence. Her presence only made me want to beat myself over the head with something blunt and heavy.<br><a href="http://s1287.photobucket.com/user/EDODonn/media/tumblr_ly4kcsAlHd1qaoevno6_250_zps13ec0593.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413291ra/813562.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_ly4kcsAlHd1qaoevno6_250_zps13ec0593.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yeah, there's some other stuff that comes up, nothing earth-shattering or important, and nothing that truly added anything to the story as a whole. It was merely filler. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Blaire reunites with her dad and finds out she has a long lost brother. Yippee. But we don't actually get to spend any time with this newly found brother so why on earth would we care that he was introduced in the first place. Dude wasn't even invited to the wedding, at least not that I know of. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Back to Nan. Oh how I hate Nan. And, aside from hating her, I wanted to punch Rush in the face every time he ran after her. I mean, come on, really? Are we really rehashing that shoddy story arc again? Didn't we suffer enough Nan in the last book? I guess not. I'd thought perhaps Nan had learned a life lesson almost getting killed and all that, sadly that seemed to only amp up her bitch-o-meter. It honestly got to the point in this book where the whole Nan/Rush relationship felt awfully incestuous. And to make matters worse, the hooker is even nastier than before. And Rush is just as big an ass, chasing her narrow ass all over L.A. while she acts like a fucktwat. And that's only when she's not screaming at Blaire and Harlow about how they've stolen everything from her and they're evil incarnate.<br><a href="http://s1287.photobucket.com/user/EDODonn/media/youstolemylife_zps021b9427.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413291ra/813563.gif" alt=" photo youstolemylife_zps021b9427.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Bitch please. Get a clue, no one cares. You suck. Please die.<br><br>So, yeah, this was an epic waste of time. There were more grammatical mistakes than I could keep track of and I found myself wincing a lot at the sentence structure. Not. Good. So, I think it's best if Abbi Glines and I part ways at this point. I'm pretty sure I'm never going to get her, and clearly, as a reader, she doesn't get me. But that's fine, she has tons of fans and my absence won't make a dent.<br><br>Farewell. I'm out.<br><a href="http://s1287.photobucket.com/user/EDODonn/media/shitshitshit_zpsfb19ae14.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413291ra/813564.gif" alt=" photo shitshitshit_zpsfb19ae14.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16567794187149080015" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=author-abbi-glines">author-abbi-glines</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer612052942" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16802201741557102889"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421094i/836160._SY540_.jpg' width='350' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Forever Too Far</i> was a <b>WILDLY</b> entertaining read. If you have enjoyed this series thus far, then you will enjoy the final installment of this series. It was a bit crazy but hey it was fun!<br/><br/>Right off the bat, be warned that <b>Nan</b> (the step-sister from hell) is still pulling her same over-the-top tantrums. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421094ra/836161.gif' width='250' height='275' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Then you have Blaire’s father’s turn-around and big reveal…<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421094i/836162.jpg' width='250' height='275' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Dean & Kiro</b>—these guys were bizarrely fun in an old rock star way. We also meet <b>Harlow</b> who is Kiro’s other daughter “the good one”.<br/><br/>Now onto </span>
  <span id="freeText16802201741557102889" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421094i/836160._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Forever Too Far</i> was a <b>WILDLY</b> entertaining read. If you have enjoyed this series thus far, then you will enjoy the final installment of this series. It was a bit crazy but hey it was fun!<br><br>Right off the bat, be warned that <b>Nan</b> (the step-sister from hell) is still pulling her same over-the-top tantrums. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421094ra/836161.gif" width="250" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then you have Blaire’s father’s turn-around and big reveal…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421094i/836162.jpg" width="250" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Dean &amp; Kiro</b>—these guys were bizarrely fun in an old rock star way. We also meet <b>Harlow</b> who is Kiro’s other daughter “the good one”.<br><br>Now onto our love story…<br><br>Blaire and Rush get through a couple of bumps: <br><br>Rush had to “relearn” the lesson that he MUST answer his damn cell phone when Blaire calls!<br><br>Rush was outright <b>SEXY</b> in this book! He can dirty talk with the best of them. Abbi Glines who writes fantastic YA, blew certain sequels of billionaire books released in the last week to shreds.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405316ra/789380.gif" width="250" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They find their hea and left me swooning while happy tears were shed.<br><br><b>
  <i>"How far is too far? I asked.<br>"It's all too far. I want you right here beside me...forever."</i>
</b><br><br>Woods fan have no fear we get a few scenes with Woods and Della! Readers should prepare for Grant/Harlow book next since we get a few chapters of their povs in this book.<br><br>Once again, I enjoyed my trip to Rosemary, Florida!</span>

<div id="review_545877817" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/545877817" />
    <a title="xrysa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9016476-xrysa"><img alt="xrysa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1438615835p2/9016476.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/545877817?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="xrysa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="xrysa" href="/user/show/9016476-xrysa">xrysa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9016476-xrysa?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer545877817" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11587095821435441557"><b>
  <blockquote>“When you find your reason for living, hold onto it. Never let it go. Even if it means burning other bridges along the way.”</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>This book made me a swooning mess.When we first met Rush he was an immature man who lived only to fuck around.Two books later and he has changed a lot.Now he has a girlfriend that he is willing to protect from everyone,including his family.Blaire is the girl that gave meaning to his life and now that they are both in love they have to face and outreach all the difficult</span>
  <span id="freeText11587095821435441557" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>“When you find your reason for living, hold onto it. Never let it go. Even if it means burning other bridges along the way.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>This book made me a swooning mess.When we first met Rush he was an immature man who lived only to fuck around.Two books later and he has changed a lot.Now he has a girlfriend that he is willing to protect from everyone,including his family.Blaire is the girl that gave meaning to his life and now that they are both in love they have to face and outreach all the difficulties that life has saved for them.<br>In this book you could say that their love is tested.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411120i/806967.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's not a secret that Nan is an egocentric,spoiled b*tch.She has always been Rush's priority but she had never respected what he loved more,<i>Blaire</i>.In this book Nan is messing around with her dad's life and since her dad is a goner perv rockstar he cant even handle her so Rush has to take action.It's wrong that Kiro(her dad) isnt trying to improve their relationship but Nan isnt helping either.She is just b*tching up all the time.There were some parts where I could totally understand her pain but overall she was a <b>DRAMA QUEEN</b><br>She pissed me off so much.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411120ra/806968.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411120ra/806969.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There was a part of me that got bored to tears!I couldnt wait for them to stop looking after Nan!I wont argue that Rush is a great brother but he unwitingly neglected the most precious thing in his life.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411120ra/806970.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Luckily,he took the right decision and he focused again on his girl.<br>From this part of the book till the end I couldnt stop swooning or smiling like an idiot.Rush is pure perfection.<br><br><i>“Blaire,<br><br>This teardrop represents many things. The tears I know you’ve shed over holding your mother’s piece of satin. The tears you’ve shed over each loss you’ve experienced. But it also represents the tears we’ve both shed as we’ve felt the little life inside you begin to move. The tears I’ve shed over the fact I’ve been given someone like you to love. I never imagined anyone like you Blaire. But every time I think about forever with you I’m humbled that you chose me.<br><br>This is your something blue.<br><br>I love you,<br><br>Rush”</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393681ra/758009.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm so glad these two people found the HEA that they both deserved.Their journey was a rollrcoster of emotions for us but in the end all the frustration and the tears were replaced by emotions of joy and happiness.<br>I still believe that the author shouldnt have written this book but it was a nice one and I cant wait for Grant's book.<br><br><b>“I’m not ever letting your sexy ass get too far away from me again.”<br>“How far is too far?” I asked.<br>“It’s all too far. I want you right here beside me… forever.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311518ra/688494.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="11587095821435441557" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer596965366" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14992288598473264683"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418600i/828996._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418600i/828997._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Before I start. If you haven't read these books at all. I can not recommend them highly enough. This are one of my absolute favourite series and I urge any contemporary romance fans to read them.<br/><br/>Moving on...<br/><br/><b>WARNING: THIS REVIEW WILL CONTAIN SPOILERS FOR BOOKS #1 & #2!</b><br/><br/>*grins*<br/><br/>*sighs*<br/><br/>Sooo, yeh... Rush. *grins and sighs*<br/><br/>*swoons*<br/><br/>Major major <i>major</i> Rush Crush over here.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418600i/828998.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*giggles*<br/><br/>Mission accomplished!<br/><br/>What is it about a super hot guy going all gooey over his baby and the mother of his child?! I don't know</span>
  <span id="freeText14992288598473264683" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418600i/828996._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418600i/828997._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Before I start. If you haven't read these books at all. I can not recommend them highly enough. This are one of my absolute favourite series and I urge any contemporary romance fans to read them.<br><br>Moving on...<br><br><b>WARNING: THIS REVIEW WILL CONTAIN SPOILERS FOR BOOKS #1 &amp; #2!</b><br><br>*grins*<br><br>*sighs*<br><br>Sooo, yeh... Rush. *grins and sighs*<br><br>*swoons*<br><br>Major major <i>major</i> Rush Crush over here.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418600i/828998.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*giggles*<br><br>Mission accomplished!<br><br>What is it about a super hot guy going all gooey over his baby and the mother of his child?! I don't know, but my God, I'm totally hot for that right now!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I love you Rush Finlay. You are going to be the best husband and father the world has ever known. One day our son's wife will be thankful that her husband will have had you for a role model. She'll be lucky because of you. Because you will have raised our son to be the man that you are. He'll love her completely because he'll know how." </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Hot hot hot. HOT. Hawt! Phew, is it hot in here?! Did I mention that Rush is pretty hot?<br><br>*melts*<br><br>This was such a perfect ending to an absolutely wonderful series. Rush has got to be in my top five book boyfriends! He is just to die for.<br><br>The way he adores Blaire, the baby, his over protectiveness... everything. Perfection, all wrapped up in the pages of a book!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I never imagined anyone like you, Blaire. But every time I think about forever with you, I'm humbled that you chose me.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Nan, I wanted to bludgeon with a blunt instrument! Jeez, does that girl not let up? Is there even a shred of humanity inside of her? Once again, this book saw her getting in between our golden couple and I wanted to stab her in the eyeballs! Bitch!<br><br>But I loved that this book didn't have any <i>major</i> angst. There were a few hiccups, some issues to overcome, but nothing too heart wrenching. Nothing was dragged out or over dramatised. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Nothing in life was as precious as this woman. It never would be. I’d found my happiness.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I loooove Abbi Glines' sex scenes. They're super duper delicious without being crude or overly done. There aren't too many of them and they are full of scrummy teasing.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Is it bad that I don't even care if someone heard us? That was too amazing to worry about anything else," she asked.<br>I lowered myself down until I could kiss her lips.<br>"They shouldn't be in my damn house is they don't want to hear us," I replied.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>It was just a cute ending to Rush and Blaire's story and it set the scene nicely for Abbi's future books; <i>Twisted Perfection</i>, Woods' book, which is sitting on my Kindle but I haven't gotten around to. The little snippets of Woods and Della, in <i>Forever Too Far</i> really made me excited to read their story. And Grant... who I assume is going to have something to do with Harlow. My only reservation about Grant's story is that I don't know how much Nan I can deal with. The girl really grates on my last nerve! So I'm hoping she simmers down a whole lot... or just pisses off altogether. That would be nice.<br><br>That's about all I have to say about this book. If you're reading this review, likelihood is, you've read the rest of the series and I'm not needing to encourage you to step into the lives of Rush and Blaire. So, I'm guessing you empathise with my Rush crush, you hate Nan as much as I do and you're feeling pretty sappy for the end of this fantastic trilogy right now. This is their HEA. Their forever.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I'm not ever letting your sexy ass get too far away from me again."<br>"How far is too far?" I asked.<br>"It's all too far. I want you right here beside me... forever."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418600i/828999._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>(I haven't created a collage for this review because I can't possibly do it without including major spoilers for the rest of the series)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389732024i/8051692._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389732024i/8051693._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>Forever Too Far</i> Statistics</b><br><b>Length</b>: 304 pages<br><b>Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥♥<br><b>Ending:</b> HEA<br><b>Series?</b> ✓ <br><b>Reading Order:</b><br>Book #1 - Fallen Too Far<br>Book #2 - Never Too Far<br>Book #3 - Forever Too Far<br>Followed by...<br>Twisted Perfection (Perfection, #1)<br>Simple Perfection (Perfection, #2) - To be released<br>And then...<br>This One Chance (Untitled Too Far Spinoff #1) - To be released<br>Take a Chance (Too Far Spinoff, #2) - To be released<br><b>Can this be read as a standalone?</b> No<br><b>Themes:</b><br>Wealth<br>Pregnancy<br>Marriage<br>Disfunctional family<br><b>Writing:</b> Great<br><br><b>AMAZON UK:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Fallen-Too-Far-ebook/dp/B00BHGQ9A6/ref=tmm_kin_title_0?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1371035539&amp;sr=8-1">http://www.amazon.co.uk/Fallen-Too-Fa...</a><br><b>AMAZON US:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Fallen-Too-Far-ebook/dp/B00BHGQ9A6/ref=tmm_kin_title_0?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1371035539&amp;sr=8-1">http://www.amazon.com/Fallen-Too-Far-...</a><br><br><b>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/529355093?book_show_action=true">Feb 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexis *Reality Bites*" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites">Alexis *Reality Bites*</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=june-july-august-2013">june-july-august-2013</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=panty-melting">panty-melting</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=discovery">discovery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer529355093" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8396086288688305029">Minor Spoilers -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br/>4 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre: New Adult Romance<br/><br/><b>River Joshua Kipling aka Captain</b><br/>The only thing I want to know is... Will we get more of shirtless Captain because he has my attention. Who names a kid River, these are things I must know.*pouts like a child* You can't just throw a curve ball like that Glines. You can't introduce me to a character and then not expand. *puts hands on hips* I need more!LOL!! Who is Captain? Read the book.<br/><br/>Ok now that </span>
  <span id="freeText8396086288688305029" style="display:none">Minor Spoilers -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br>4 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: New Adult Romance<br><br><b>River Joshua Kipling aka Captain</b><br>The only thing I want to know is... Will we get more of shirtless Captain because he has my attention. Who names a kid River, these are things I must know.*pouts like a child* You can't just throw a curve ball like that Glines. You can't introduce me to a character and then not expand. *puts hands on hips* I need more!LOL!! Who is Captain? Read the book.<br><br>Ok now that I got that out of the way can I just say I loved this book! I think the fact that Abbi Glines will be putting out stories for her other characters involved in this story has caused her to not give us an epilogue that is most desired. But whatever I still enjoyed this book!<br><br><b>She’s a bitch. I know it. You know it. And she knows it. Nan.</b><br>After finding out who her real birth father is Nan decides to raise hell. Dean comes to get Rush so that he can muzzle the mangy redheaded mutt who has been causing chaos at his home in California. But don't they know she can't be tamed? <br><br>How many times must you try to help Nan, Rush? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408630ra/799527.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m3jgnqI7Zo1qzhj33o1_500_zps0a67df15.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How many? Inquiring minds want to know.<br><br><i>
  <b>'I knew what it felt like to have a father not want you. But I also knew what it felt like to have a father who adored you. She didn’t.'</b>
</i> -Blaire<br><br><br>Our sweet Blaire supports Rush and decides to go to California with him. BIG MISTAKE. HUGE. You wanna know what Rush does once they get to Cali? Chase after Nan that's what. Rush has been playing the father figure for his baby sister for so long that it just comes natural. Much to the dismay of his fiancee Blaire who starts to wonder if he will ever put her first.<br><br>Rush does put Blaire first eventually just not before a bunch of bullshit involving Nan and her over the top drama swallows him whole.<br><br>Nan has a one tracked mine with a few stations to change it up but her main station is<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759771.gif" alt=" photo IdontgiveaF_zps4bbde43c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Which leads me to wonder...<br><br>Does Nan get a book? I hope not I can't stand her she needs to grow the f*ck up and stop playing the blame game. Daddy don't love me. Mommy don't love me, nobody loves me. Really Bit*h? MOVE ON. GET OVER IT. How long is she willing to let that crap<u> define her</u>. <br><b>HA, you know what?</b><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408630i/799528.jpg" alt=" photo 9568fbba-9c23-4caa-b980-56266c0168a1_zps41abb37c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Moving on.<br><br>Grant. Where to start? I want him. Oh no wait, I mean I want his book! Being in Grants head gave me a<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408630ra/799529.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lwtlzaffXe1qiagt5_zps382651d0.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Did anyone else experience this too? And Naturally I had to have this book immediately. IMMEDIATELY! I almost couldn't get internet access to have ti downloaded and I nearly died a thousand deaths, but I got it, I started it, and I f</span>
  <span id="freeText4333212546647274141" style="display:none"><b>Update: FULL REVIEW-19/06/2013</b><br><br><i>
  <b>“When you find your reason for living, hold onto it. Never let it go. Even if it means burning other bridges along the way.”</b>
</i> -Rush<br><br>Ok so! Where do I even start with this review. As you all know, I'm a huge Abbi fan...like huge. Massive girl crush on the lady huge! Yeah. And Naturally I had to have this book immediately. IMMEDIATELY! I almost couldn't get internet access to have ti downloaded and I nearly died a thousand deaths, but I got it, I started it, and I finished....IN ONE DAY! Yeah, that's how awesome this book, it's a wonderful ending to the perfect love story.<br><br>We get our duel narrative again in here from both Rush and Blaire and it was just so fantastic to be back with these two amazing people, that I just simply couldn't put it down. Forever Too Far follows on from the events of Never Too Far, and picks up with Rush and Blaire trying to work through their past issues and move on. (Trying to write this without spoilers is difficult).<br><br>Not only do we pick up with Rush and Blaire, but we get the full extent of them trying to deal with the bitch that is Rush sister Nan. She's raising hell and Rush has to jump in try and calm her down. Pfffft. Good luck Rush! Abbi has a real knack for introducing new characters and we get a couple of new characters and his brother Grant makes a more prominent appearance in the book which is fantastic, Abbi's secondary characters are all pretty well written and all have apart to play in the book and the lives of Rush and Blaire. <br><br>The thing about this book is you think that you've got plenty, and then BAM Abbi introduces new characters and adds a couple of narratives from Grant and that's it. You're done, you're hooked, you want more. And I do. I honestly can't wait to get into Grants head more, and I already love that Harlow will be his love interest, that's really going to interesting to say the least, for all sorts of reasons which I won't say because it's a spoiler. <br><br>Overall Forever Too Far was a perfect ending to Rush and Blaire. Their loose ends were tied up, they got their HEA and, even though there was no epilogue it was still perfect, and it's a trilogy that is going to stay with me for a long time like all of Abbi's books do. It's wonderful and I'm telling you, if you haven't picked up the series yet, then you really should. Be sure to read Twisted Perfection (Woods Story) before this one otherwise you'll get spoilers you don't want for Forever Too Far. <br><br><i>
  <b>Note:</b>
</i> <i>This is NOT YA. This book is only suitable for ages 17+ due to adult themes and sexual content.</i><br><br>I'm just going to leave you with some quotes from this fabulous book.<br><br><b>

<span id="freeTextContainer7972724750207597286">This is <i>it</i>...the final story of Blaire and Rush and whether or not they will get their Happily Ever After. It really is bittersweet for those of us with Rush Crushes. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/502443.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I can remember the moment when I first read about Rush and just knew he would be the one for Blaire.   <span id="freeText7972724750207597286" style="display:none">This is <i>it</i>...the final story of Blaire and Rush and whether or not they will get their Happily Ever After. It really is bittersweet for those of us with Rush Crushes. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/502443.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I can remember the moment when I first read about Rush and just knew he would be the one for Blaire. It has been a great ride reading about all their trials and tribulations and seeing them come together and work things out. <br><br>Is everything roses? No, of course not...Rush still makes some of the same mistakes but...he is working on it and getting better at focusing on his priorities. <br><br>The old gun toting "Alabama", I mean Blaire, is back and I loved it. I kind of missed her in <i>Never Too Far</i>. And yes, she is still running but just like Rush, she is maturing and figuring out what's important too. <br><br>Besides Rush and Blaire, I felt like the main focus of this book was family. I loved how ~almost~ everyone was coming together. The holidays were really special and we even get to meet a new character. Well, make that two! <br><br>Of course, Nan is still the wicked witch. Ugh...Don't get me wrong, I can't stand her but now things have just gotten sad. I really feel sorry for her. I was hoping that with everything she went through that maybe she would get a clue. I don't think we will hear from her much in <i>Simple Perfection</i>, (no, we have the awful Angelina to contend with there...don't even get me started on her!) but unfortunately, she will definitely be in Grant's books. I would like to hate her a little less....just a little. I just felt it was too much!<br><br>Back to happier, and <i>sexier</i> things....I love sexy Rush and his tongue piercing! ~sigh~ Rush and Blaire have some really great steamy scenes and his dirty mouth is to die for but I LOVE romantic Rush!! There are sooo many sweet things he did. I wish I could talk about them but I don't want to spoil it for you. Let's just say if you find a man that does these things for you, DON'T LET HIM GO!! <br><br>(and I love their song.....<a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jpYJNhLrey8" rel="nofollow noopener">The "♥" song</a>)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379792834i/569075.png" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One word of advice if you are going to read the spin off series, read <i>Twisted Perfection</i> before this book. Abbi Glines has recommend to do the same on her blog because there are some spoilers for Woods story if you don't. <br><br>Overall, I am happy with the way things ended. I will miss Rush and Blaire but I know we will get tidbits in the last Woods book and of course, in Grant's books....and I can't wait! <br><br><br>Favorite quotes: <br><br>♥ “When you find your reason for living, hold onto it. Never let it go. Even if it means burning other bridges along the way.”<br><br>♥ “Sweet Blaire, I’m not one to sit back and enjoy the action. I prefer to experience the action. Watching football does not compete with getting you naked and under me.”<br><br>♦ “I really wish I could confirm to him that you do in fact have a penis. That hurts its feelings.”<br><br>♥ ♫ ♪ <i>I’ll give you a new name<br>nothing in life will be the same <br>the story is now complete <br>our life and love is all we need   <br>‘Cause I couldn’t help from falling falling for you</i> ♪ ♫<br><br>♥ "I think I may have come in my damn jeans when you told her you could pierce her ears from there. I’m f*cking that sweet little bad*ss p*ssy tonight.”<br><br>♥ “How far is too far?” I asked.<br><br>“It’s all too far. I want you right here beside me... forever.”</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4921695905081906557"><b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/>To be perfectly honest, I vacillated many, many times as to how to rate this book. Finally, after sleeping on it and thinking about it, I finally settled for 3.5. I wish I could give this one a solid 4 or even a 5 but there were too many things that bothered me. <br/><br/>Anyway, onto the review. Let's start with the good first. <br/><br/><a target='_blank' title='ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting' href='http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/33/blackandwhitecouplecutet.jpg/' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText4921695905081906557" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars</b><br><br>To be perfectly honest, I vacillated many, many times as to how to rate this book. Let's start with the good first. <br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/33/blackandwhitecouplecutet.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419126i/830572.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><u>Rush and Blaire</u><br>I'm glad these two finally had their HEA. Loved the first book, didn't care for the second one, and this time, Rush and Blaire had me swooning once again. Well, at least, when they weren't doing anything stupid like running off without talking it out with your partner!!(Yes, I'm talking to you Blaire!) Anyway, more on that later but seriously, you guys, I loved <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[their wedding especially when Rush serenaded Blaire as she walked down the aisle. <i>*sigh*</i> And when Rush gave Blaire her something old, something new, something borrowed and something blue, I was swooned!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> That was the highlight for me. I wish there were more of that, which totally sucked. <br><br><u>The "teaser" POVs</u><br>Yes, we get two teaser POVs. I say teaser because we get to read these POVs twice each, I think. I will not say who these POVs belong to but one thing for sure, these two will be getting their own books soon. :DD<br><br><u>The writing</u><br>Another factor that I enjoyed in this book is the writing. Abbi Glines has a way with keeping the readers glued to the book, forsaking food and even sleep until the book is finished. Heck, I could not put this book down. Her writing style just sucked me right in. Plus, she certainly knows how to infuse steam into her books, which is always a plus for me. <br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/708/tumblrmcbcrpt9as1qkoifq.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419126i/830573.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Now, let's go into the not-so-pleasant things in this book...<br><br>First off, Nan. Enough said. She just went from bad to worse and I have a feeling, we haven't seen the last of her drama. Apparently, Nan has to continue to be a first-class bitch for this story to progress. It was just too much and she was saying the same thing over and over and over again. :( <br><br>I also wasn't happy when my suspicions were confirmed about Grant and Nan having something-something on the side. Argh! There better be some good explanation for this! <br><br>Second, Rush totally buying Nan's bullshit for nth time and Blaire running off with talking it out with Rush. I mean seriously?? That was just annoying. <br><br>Third, the abrupt ending. Not even going into that one. I wanted a freaking grand epilogue, okay! I could care less about Woods and Della! They're going to have their own book! WTH!! I was totally bummed!<br><br><br>Fans of Abbi Glines will no doubt love this one. The things I mentioned above are personal and as I have said, I enjoyed reading it in spite of the issues. Peace!<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="4921695905081906557" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

This should be their happily ever after, but is it really? Or will Rush continue to put Blaire and his son second? Blaire isn't sure if Nan will finally get what she </span>
  <span id="freeText744239522600778314" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420823i/835273.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>♥♥♥ 3 Stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424809i/847133._SY540_.jpg" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"When you find your reason for living, hold onto it. Never let it go. Even if it means burning other bridges along the way."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Blaire and Rush are together and things seem to moving in the right direction. This should be their happily ever after, but is it really? Or will Rush continue to put Blaire and his son second? Blaire isn't sure if Nan will finally get what she wants and end the relationship she has with Rush. The question is, can she live without him? Or will they get their forever?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424809i/847134._SY540_.jpg" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“She is everything I want to be."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I love you, Rush Finlay. You are going to be the best husband and father the world has ever known."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Can I just say that Rush was so freaking AWESOME in this book! Gah! He made me swoon and sigh SO MUCH! Even though he was kinda stupid sometimes, falling for the same crap over again, I still loved him! He is the best father ever. He was so funny how overprotective he became. But he was also so sweet and just amazing! OMG his friggin song! I went on a SWOON and SIGH overload. I'm glad I decided to listen to it when it showed up in the book. If you want to listen to it (which I am sure you will want to do), click on the link below:<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jpYJNhLrey8">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jpYJNh...</a><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424809i/847135.jpg" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I love you, Blaire. I'm so damn proud of the fact you're going to be the mother of my son. I want everyone to know. Never doubt that."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Blaire was kinda a dumb in this book, well, specifically in one part. It was all a misunderstanding. Had she stayed and talked it out, things would have been different. But still, I love how badass she can be. She also was so supportive and caring to Rush, no matter how she was feeling. Blaire, she was one awesome mommy. Seeing her and Rush interact with their child was so freaking sweet! I LOVED it! It made me smile so much and feel all warm and fuzzy.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/635694.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What ruined this book for me, was a certain person. You know who I'm talking about. I'm talking about the "one who should not be named", and no it's not Voldemort. It's Nan. I still don't like her, and I don't even feel sorry for her. I just plain LOATHE her. I'm sure my opinion will never change. She continued to be a bitch and tried to manipulate Rush. I was hoping she would change, but now even if she did, I still wouldn't like her.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/467389.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Another thing that didn't fit well into the story for me, was that Blaire's father had another BIG secret! I was completely blindsided. I was not expecting it. I mean, how many freaking secrets does he have? It was a bit odd for me and really only to be mentioned a few times in the book. It seemed rather unimportant to even mention it. But maybe Abbi is planning a book on that.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/582902.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I love you, Rush Finlay."<br>"Good 'cause I'm not ever letting your sexy ass get too far away from me again."<br>"How far is too far?" I asked.<br>"It's all too far. I want you right here beside me....forever."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Anyways, the book was a sweet good read. It was a good ending for Blaire and Rush. There were a lot of such great moments. I definitely felt so happy for the new member of their family. But the actual ending of this book, was rather abrupt. I was kinda left thinking "This is it? Am I missing pages?" I just felt like there was some stuff added to this book to make it interesting, unfortunately I didn't find it that way. Still, it was a good read, and if you are a hardcore Rush and Blaire fan, you should definitely check it out.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9633653096833955924">It definitely could have been better. I think we all would have liked a little less Nan, but overall I am glad that Abbi Glines decided to listen to her fans and write this. I think it was a lovely ending for Blair and Rush and after it stopped focusing so much on Nan it was really sweet and cute. I am really excited now for Grants story even though I know that means that I am going to have to hear more about Nan... GAG!!!!   <span id="freeText9633653096833955924" style="display:none">It definitely could have been better. I think we all would have liked a little less Nan, but overall I am glad that Abbi Glines decided to listen to her fans and write this. I think it was a lovely ending for Blair and Rush and after it stopped focusing so much on Nan it was really sweet and cute. I am really excited now for Grants story even though I know that means that I am going to have to hear more about Nan... GAG!!!! Harlow similarly to Della seems like a character you can't help but to instantly love. I am glad to have gotten a sneak peak of what to expect there. I am also looking forward to the follow up to Twisted Perfection. I really enjoyed that one. Overall, I think Abbi Glines books get better the more she writes them... for the most part anyway. I will remain a loyal fan because as I have said in the past there is something about her books that is just comforting it's a guilty pleasure that you know will stir up your emotions but not too much. Let's face it; we don't always need that life changing sticks with you for weeks &amp; months type of book. Sometimes you just need a quick story, with some hot sex, and a glass of wine to escape to for a little while. Abbi Glines is the queen of that. If I am in a book funk I know I can turn to an Abbi Glines book to help settle me down and help me move on to the next story. Thumbs up, and so long Blair &amp; Rush you guys were great. </span>

My saving grace is the hope that Nan will be dealt with all proper like in Grant’s book. Are you there, Abbi? It’s me, Jen! Please give Nan the figurative bitch slapping she deserves and soon!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10913217210904779477">I felt like they matured in this book, progressed in their relationship and transitioned into fully functioning adults. Loved the insight into Della and Woods' story, interesting tidbit there at the end. <br/>I felt like Rush finally started taking Blaires side (TOOK YOU LONG ENOUGH) and he made obvious strides in his relationship with Nan, by -at the end - putting her in her place, it was also interesting to see Grant and Harlows perspective at certain points in the book, I was worried when reading </span>
  <span id="freeText10913217210904779477" style="display:none">I felt like they matured in this book, progressed in their relationship and transitioned into fully functioning adults. Loved the insight into Della and Woods' story, interesting tidbit there at the end. <br />I felt like Rush finally started taking Blaires side (TOOK YOU LONG ENOUGH) and he made obvious strides in his relationship with Nan, by -at the end - putting her in her place, it was also interesting to see Grant and Harlows perspective at certain points in the book, I was worried when reading the first teaser that Harlow was going to be a problem for Blaire and Rush but she turned out to be a nice friend for Blaire and someone who hated Nan equally.<br />Personally although I thought Kiro was a self indulgent asshole, I felt like Nan brought it on herself with all her shrieking and whining... I also thought what she did the day in the hotel was ridiculous and she wasnt doing it seriously, she did it for attention - or she wouldnt have phoned Rush.<br />Altogether I really enjoyed the book, the writing was fantastic, the characters were engaging, the plot was the perfect levels of drama and fluffy romance :D<br /><br />-----------------------------------------------------<br /><b> TEASERS 2 + 3 from book blogs </b><br /><br />Kiro was shirtless and swinging his tattooed arms around with a cigarette between his fingers and a bottle of rum in his other hand. “What the ever loving f*ck is your problem? Hell, you got momma issues then go bitch at mother f*cking Georgianna. Why am I the one being dealt this crazy shit?” Kiro was yelling at Nan when I walked into the game room. A pair of black lace panties were on the pool table but the female I’d left him with a few hours earlier was nowhere to be seen. Small miracles.<br />“Rush! Do you hear him? He doesn’t care about me. He doesn’t care that he ignored me most of my life and do you know he has a daughter? Some uptight bitch that won’t even look at me.” Nan was still screaming.<br />I walked over to her and grabbed both her hands. “Take a couple deep breaths, Nan. You gotta calm down so we can all talk. You yelling isn’t gonna fix shit.”<br />She glared at me but did as I told her to. I waited until she’d taken two deep breaths before squeezing her hands. “Good. Now, go sit over there on that sofa and don’t talk. Let me talk. Okay?”<br />She frowned but nodded her head and walked over to the white leather sectional sofa that outlined two of the four walls in this room. Once she was seated I turned back around to look at Kiro. He was taking another long swig from the rum. The man needed to stop drinking and eat something. You could see his ribs. His fetish with leather went beyond furniture. He wore it too. The leather pants he had on were hanging on his tattooed hipbones.<br />“Can’t believe you got her to shut up for a whole damn minute,” Kiro muttered and put the cigarette back to his lips.<br /><br /><br />------------------------------------------------------<br /><br />The night breeze was cold now. I immediately shivered and Rush stopped and wrapped his arms around me. “We need to go to the house. I’m not going to make her stand out here and talk. It’s too damn cold.” Rush told his father. <br /><br />Dean finally stopped walking and looked back at me. His eyes slowly took me in and I could see the moment he noticed my stomach. <br /><br />“Dean, this is Blaire Wynn. My fiancée. Blaire this is Dean Finlay, my father.” Rush said in a tight voice. He didn’t sound like he wanted to make this introduction. <br /><br />“No one told me I was gonna be a grandpa,” he said in a slow drawl. I wasn’t sure how he felt about that because there was no emotion on his face. <br /><br />“I’ve been busy,” was the only response Rush gave him. That was odd. Was he embarrassed to tell his dad? I felt sick at my stomach and started to ease away from him. <br /><br />His arms tightened their hold on me and I could feel his attention focused completely on me. “What’s wrong?” He asked turning his back on his father and bending down so he could look me directly in the eyes. <br /><br />I didn’t want to have this conversation in front of Dean. I could feel his dad’s eyes on both of us. I shook my head but my body was still tense. I couldn’t help that. The fact he hadn’t told his father was bothering me. <br /><br />“I’m taking her to the car. I’ll meet you back at the house,” Rush said over his shoulder but kept his eyes focused on mine. I dropped my gaze wishing I hadn’t reacted now. I was making a scene. Dean was going to think I was a whinny princess. <br /><br />----------------------------------------------------------------<br /><br />For more reviews please check out <a href="http://beckasbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">My Blog</a></span>

  <span id="freeText17678075075408726523" style="display:none">I'm giving this 4 stars just because I love Rush and Blaire. Honestly I'm a bit disappointed with this 'last' book, you know the feeling when you love the first book so much you get too excited and you expect TOO MUCH on the next books? that's what happen too me..I expected too much but in end it felt like it did not meet my expectations. There's hardly any conflict in this book, it's just the same psychoNan drama, Blaire running away Rush chasing her, promising this and that and then sex and sex.<br />I do still love this book, atleast we get to see Nate and in some way Rush and Blaire's relationship matured.<br />I guess my mixed feelings for these books started because of my disappointment over Della (yep! Della) I don't know, I just hate how Woods' book turned out and he ended up with Della, don't think she's heroine material and good enough for Woods.There it all started I got so disappointed and then you add the unspeakable Nan/Grant pairing I was like "WTH Abbi Glines"<br /><br />On the positive note here are the things I love about this book..Harlow, Harlow, Harlow!!!! Thank God!!! I thought the petition against Nan was hopeless..thank God Abbi took pity..Grant! I am so looking forward to your book. Now it makes me wonder if Abbi did plan this all along or she really intended Grant to end up with Nan at first but then changed her mind because of all the fans' violent reactions..LOL! <div id="review_596617785" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

        <a title="★★Sara Lizzy★★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="★★Sara Lizzy★★" href="/user/show/17083195-sara-lizzy">★★Sara Lizzy★★</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17083195-sara-lizzy?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17083195-sara-lizzy?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>
