        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer596617785" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer551820769787358612"><b>5 STARS!</b><br/><br/>This review contains spoilers! Also if you haven't read Woods' book <i>Twisted Perfection</i>, I'd strongly suggest you do so before reading this book. This book gives away spoilers from things that happened in Woods' book!<br/><br/><b>"When you find your reason for living, hold onto it. Never let it go. Even if it means burning other bridges along the way."</b> ~Rush Finlay<br/><br/>When the book starts off Rush and Blaire are in a bar with Woods and other people when Rush notices his dad, Dean Finlay (notorious drummer</span>
  <span id="freeText551820769787358612" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS!</b><br /><br />This review contains spoilers! Also if you haven't read Woods' book <i>Twisted Perfection</i>, I'd strongly suggest you do so before reading this book. This book gives away spoilers from things that happened in Woods' book!<br /><br /><b>"When you find your reason for living, hold onto it. Never let it go. Even if it means burning other bridges along the way."</b> ~Rush Finlay<br /><br />When the book starts off Rush and Blaire are in a bar with Woods and other people when Rush notices his dad, Dean Finlay (notorious drummer of Slacker Demon) walk in. Rush and Blaire lead him outside to talk away from all the people around. Rush introduces Blaire to his dad and it's then that Dean notices Blaire is pregnant.<br /><br /><b>"No one told me I was gonna be a grandpa," he said in a slow drawl. I wasn't sure how he felt about that because there was no emotion on his face.<br />"I've been busy," was the only response Rush gave him.</b><br /><br />Blaire felt sick over the idea that Rush hadn't told his dad about her or the baby. Rush could sense a change in Blaire, and told his dad he was taking Blaire to the car and he could meet them at the house, since Blaire wouldn't tell Rush what was wrong in front of his father. When they get in the car, Rush asks Blaire again what's wrong so he can fix it. She asks why he hasn't told his dad about her.<br /><br /><b>"I haven't taken time to track him down. And I knew he'd show up when I told him because he'd want to meet you. I wasn't ready for company just yet. Especially him."<br />________<br /><br />"He's here now. So, let's go see what brought him here before my mother finds out. I want you to myself. I don't like having my fucked up family around."</b><br /><br />Rush knew that since his dad didn't know about Blaire and he showed up there to see Rush, that it could very well be about Nan. <br /><br /><b>"I love you, Blaire. I'm so damn proud of the fact you're going to be the mother of my son. I want everyone to know. Never doubt that."</b><br /><br />When they arrive home Rush gets right to the point with his dad.<br /><br /><b>"Now, why're you here?"<br />"What? Can't a dad come see his son when he wants to?"<br />"It's Rosemary. You never come here."<br />Dean shrugged and took a swig of his beer, then threw an arm over the back of the sofa and propped both his feet up on the coffee table. "Your sister is a crazy bitch. She's <i>fucking insane.</i>. We need help."<br />"What's has Nan done?"<br />"Question is, what hasn't she done. Damn girl is raising hell. We can't get any rest. We finished up the tour two weeks ago and came back to LA to enjoy some down time. She showed up and all hell broke loose. No one is getting any down time. Kiro doesn't know what to do with her. We need help."<br />"Is she staying at the mansion?" I asked.<br />Dad raised his eyebrows. "Do I look like an idiot to you? Fuck no, she isn't staying there. She just shows up all the damn time. She's making demands and shit. Kiro has tried to smooth things over and form some sort of relationship with her but she won't let him. She won't listen and she.... well, she found out he has another daughter. Didn't go over well."</b><br /><br />Blaire tells Rush he should go help her see if she can form some sort of relationship with Kiro. Rush wants to disagree, but his dad cuts him off and says that both Rush and Blaire should come back to LA so he can get to know Blaire.<br /><br />When Dean asks when the baby is due and when the wedding is. Blaire says she's 20 weeks along. She says they were going to marry in 2 weeks but she'd rather put it off so it's not weighing on Rush and let him deal with his family issues first. Rush hated that idea. He wanted to get married and he hated her being Blaire Wynn while their baby grew inside her. He wanted her to have his name and everyone to know that he wants her and his baby.<br /><br />They end up waiting until after Thanksgiving until they go to LA. It's the first time Rush has ever had an actual turkey dinner for Thanksgiving. And he surprises Blaire by making arrangements for her dad to fly in for the holiday too. It's Blaire's first Thanksgiving without her mom and she's happy to have her dad there.<br /><br />Dean tells Rush that Grant had been dating Nan for awhile. Rush is upset that Grant never told him about it, so he calls Grant to confront him. Grant says that part of him was falling in love with Nan. He said that Nan was done with him and he's not going to play her games anymore.<br /><br />After Blaire's dad heads back to Florida after Thanksgiving, Rush, Blaire and Dean head for LA. To make a long story short- Nan is her usual bitchy self, not only is it directed at Harlow (Kiro's other daughter), she's bitchy with Blaire because she thinks Blaire got pregnant on purpose, says Blaire is taking Rush away from her. She even goes as far as to tell Rush one night when she's upset that Blaire was picking on her at the dinner table in front of everyone when Rush was in the other room, even though it was Nan initiating the argument and Blaire was only defending herself and her baby. Rush believed Nan, which really pissed me off. Blaire never really got an opportunity to tell Rush what really happened because he had to keep running off after Nan. Nan ended up threatening to end her life twice. The second time she threatened to end her life, Blaire and Rush were in the middle of an argument because Rush was so stressed over everything, he was taking his frustrations out on her at the time, he got a phone call from Nan saying good-bye. Of course, Rush goes off to help Nan. Meanwhile back at the mansion, Blaire has been having cramping and she just thought it was stress, she's seen so little of Rush she didn't get a chance to tell him about it. When she's out with Harlow by the pool she has severe enough cramping that she ends up crying. Harlow convinces her to go to her doctor to get checked. When she's at the doctor's office, she notices she's bleeding slightly.<br /><br />While this is happening Rush is at the hotel Nan is at, trying to get Nan to answer the door, when that doesn't work, he has someone let him in. Nan had overdosed. He's getting a phone call from Harlow at the same time the paramedics are there, and because he blames Nan's stress partly on Harlow at the time, he doesn't answer it and throws his cell phone across the room. When he goes in the ambulence with Nan, he doesn't have his phone with. <br /><br />The doctors keep Blaire for observation for awhile, she's unable to reach Rush and neither is Harlow. When she's released, she's supposed to stay away from stress, and make sure she's eating and drinking and getting rest. She's so hurt that Rush didn't answer her texts that she calls her dad and asks if she can come stay with him in Florida on his boat. The dad agrees, and she sneaks off and catches the first plane out. <br /><br />Rush calls his mom to come care for Nan, realizing FINALLY that he cannot help Nan anymore and he has his own family he needs to care for now, he also tells the doctors that he thinks Nan needs to be admitted somewhere after her suicide attempt. He goes back to the hotel and finds his phone and all the missed texts from Blaire and one from Harlow saying that she took Blaire to the doctor and she's cramping and bleeding. Rush freaks out because he can't believe he wasn't there for Blaire. As he's rushing home, he calls Blaire's phone and it goes directly to voicemail, so he calls Harlow. Harlow said that Blaire never came down to dinner and when she knocked on her door to bring her a plate of food, she didn't answer so Harlow left her alone to sleep. Rush told her to open the door and check on her.<br /><br />When Rush gets back to the mansion, his dad and Harlow are in the foyer and he knows something is wrong. They tell him Blaire took off and left no note behind. Rush is panicking and trying to figure out why she'd just leave him without letting him know. <br /><br /><b>I shook my head and walked inside. "Gone? She can't be gone! Where would she go?"<br />"Probably somewhere so she doesn't have to deal with Nan's shit and her fiance running off and leaving her and not answering her damn calls. That'd be my guess. You're a stupid fucker, just like me, son," Dean said with disgust in his voice before walking away.</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>She was gone. Every little trace of Blaire was gone. She'd needed me. Our baby had needed me and I'd been with Nan, again. I deserve to be left.<br />I closed the door behind me before leaning against the wall and sliding down to the floor to weep. The fear of losing Nan had been terrifying but the idea of losing Blaire and my baby was unbearable. I didn't deserve Blaire. I had promised her I'd always be there yet my family kept pulling me away. It was time I stopped letting that happen. But what if I was too late?<br />I shook my head and wiped the tears from my face. I'd find her and I'd beg. I'd grovel. Whatever I needed to do I would do it. Then I'd never leave her again. For anyone.</i>
</b><br /><br />Rush ends up calling Blaire and she agrees to let him come down to Florida and spend time with her and her dad. Blaire meets a guy in his twenties they call Captain there. It's later revealed that Captain has a connection to Blaire's dad <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Her dad had a baby that was given up for adoption when Blaire's dad was 16 year's old- "Captain" is that boy that was given away- he's Blaire's half-brother <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Rush is determined to marry Blaire when they return to Rosemary. He gives her 1 week before they will marry. Rush was so romantic when he'd send up gifts for her something old, something new, something borrowed and something blue and the notes to go with them. Then the wedding was so romantic also. I was amazed at everything Rush had planned. They plan to go to his penthouse in Manhattan for their honeymoon. Blaire had never been to New York so it was a new adventure for her, but they also wanted the comfort of home and her obstetrician was going to set Blaire up with one there to check on her while they were away.<br /><br />The book eventually skips ahead 3 months. Rush and Blaire are back in Rosemary. Blaire is about ready to give birth, she's due any day. Her water breaks in the club parking lot after she was there visiting. Luckily Rush was there playing golf with Grant so he was nearby to drive her to the hospital. She gave birth to a boy named Nathan Rush Finlay, or "Nate" for his nickname. It was cute how possessive Rush was of Nate and didn't want anyone else to hold him or be near him when they were at the hospital.<br /><br />As time goes on, eventually Nan shows up at Rush and Blaire's house. Rush is gone with Grant and Blaire lets Nan in out of respect for Rush since it's his sister. She's a total bitch and says Nate probably isn't even Rush's baby. Blaire is mad. She ends up leaving to go get her phone to call Rush, who immediately returns home when he learns Nan is there and isn't being polite to Blaire. Blaire goes to get Nate and is about to walk down the beach with him when Rush asks Blaire to bring the Nate in so Nan can see him. Blaire is really unsure about the whole thing but Rush assures her.<br /><br /><b>"If you want me to take him and you not go in there I will. But if you want to go in there I swear to you that she will behave or I'll throw her out of this house."</b><br /><br />Blaire agrees to take Nate in with Rush to see Nan reluctantly. When Nan spun around to look at Nate, Blaire saw the moment she realized that each small feature was Rush's. Then she turns into a real bitch and I was really proud of how Rush handled it.<br /><br /><b>"Guess he is yours after all," she said. I stopped and took a step back bumping into Rush's chest. His arm came around me and he held me there.<br />"You wanted to see him. Be careful what you say to his mother. Apologize for that last stupid ass remark or I'm going to walk you to the door."<br />Nan's eyes flared with fury and I had a feeling Rush had just started something we really didn't need in our home. But he took a deep breath and lifted her hate filled eyes to me. "I'm sorry," she snapped. She didn't mean it but the fact Rush had made her say it was worth it.<br />"Can I hold him?" Nan asked, lifting her gaze to Rush's.<br />I went stiff as a board. If he told her yes I was marking a run for it with Nate. There was only so much he could ask of me.<br />"Probably not a good idea. With you glaring at his momma like that I don't think she's gonna feel safe handing him over."<br />Nan scowled. "He's your kid too."<br />"He is. But Blaire is his mother. I don't let anything happen that she isn't comfortable with."<br />"God, Rush where did your balls go?"<br />"That's strike two, sis."<br />"I just wanted to see the kid and let you know I'm doing better. If you want to see me I'm in town for a few days. I'm not up for anymore bonding with your little family here so keep that in mind."</b><br /><br />That's not where the story ends, but you can read it to see what happens from there. I was happy that after all Nan's drama in LA, Rush learned to put Blaire and Nate first. He never made that mistake again of putting anyone before them.<br /><br /><b>"I love you, Rush Finlay."<br />"Good 'cause I'm never letting your sexy ass get too far away from me again."<br />"How far is too far?" I asked.<br />"It's all too far. I want you right here beside me....forever."</b><br /><br />This book has brief appearances by Woods and Della and Woods' ex, which is why if you haven't read Woods' book <i>Twisted Perfection</i> yet, I suggest you do so. This book alternates POV between Rush and Blaire but also has 3 different points in the book where it was either Grant's or Harlow's POV. To be honest, that's why it took me so long to decide what to rate this book. I loved the book, but it was supposed to be Rush and Blaire's book and I didn't like having Grant and Harlow's POV thrown into it when it didn't involve Rush or Blaire in anyway. I felt that if the author wanted us to have a sneak peek at Grant and Harlow's situation, then a sneak peek of Grant's book should have been added in AFTER this book was done. That's why I had such a hard time deciding whether or not to reduce my rating because of that, but ultimately- I decided to leave it at 5 stars which is what I would have given it if their POV wasn't in Rush and Blaire's book anyway- the only reason I did that is because Abbi never intended on having this 3rd book for Rush and Blaire, she was going to stop after the 2nd book- she wrote it for the fans of the series. I figured I wasn't going to deduct for such a minor thing when she went out of her way for the fans of the series to write this 3rd book. I was annoyed with Nan throughout the book also, but she's always been a part of this series and I knew what to expect from her, so I wasn't going to let my irritation over her affect my rating either. I was happy that Rush and Blaire got their HEA and that's all that mattered in the end for me. Well that and the fact that Rush finally figured out Blaire and his baby should come first for him.</span>
  <a data-text-id="551820769787358612" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_637344734" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/637344734" />
    <a title="Angela Richardson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14805495-angela-richardson"><img alt="Angela Richardson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459652982p2/14805495.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/637344734?book_show_action=true">Jun 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela Richardson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela Richardson" href="/user/show/14805495-angela-richardson">Angela Richardson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer637344734" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2966072812129062882">3 stars. <br/>Am not gonna lie... I struggled to give it 3 stars. <br/><br/>To be honest, I think I lost a lot of my Rush Crush after the first book. He wasn't as cool as he used to be, and he has lost a lot of that original bad boy demeanor I use to find so hot from the first book. It's been going steadily downhill for me in these last two books, and although he is very lovey-dovey with Blair, it wasn't what I liked about him in the first place. He has lost A LOT of edge. Perhaps it's from the way he chases a</span>
  <span id="freeText2966072812129062882" style="display:none">3 stars. <br />Am not gonna lie... I struggled to give it 3 stars. <br /><br />To be honest, I think I lost a lot of my Rush Crush after the first book. He wasn't as cool as he used to be, and he has lost a lot of that original bad boy demeanor I use to find so hot from the first book. It's been going steadily downhill for me in these last two books, and although he is very lovey-dovey with Blair, it wasn't what I liked about him in the first place. He has lost A LOT of edge. Perhaps it's from the way he chases after Blaire, but this book sunk my crush for him - big time! . Sorry Rush boy! my Rush Crush has been tossed to the wind! I also would have liked to have seen Blaire do a bit of chasing or begging for once too! Or an epic fight between them! Something that was better than this flat lined effect I felt whilst reading this one.<br /> <br />OH, and I was really annoyed that Blaire up and left Rush after not hearing from him on that 'one day'. I mean - I get she was disappointed and scared, but she is engaged to the guy and should have at least heard him out before she hopped on a plane and ran away. Bit dramatic and immature Blaire don't you think! I just hated that he wasn't angry she stuck around to at least 'talk' it out before running off. That really pushed it down further for me.<br /> <br />And then there was the storyline which just felt weak. So weak.<br />NAN!? That could have been wiped from the book completely and I wouldn't have noticed. And the other sweet moments &amp; scenes were not enough to hold my attention - even with the intertwining of the other characters. <br /><br />And the ending. Ugggghhhhh. Awful. I kinda wish I had Blaire's gun in that final scene with her at the end so I could have used it on myself - (harsh but true) <br />So,<br />Would I read it again - ummm - that's a solid NO.<br />would I recommend it - only to really (and I'm talking hardcore) die hard Rush fans. Am sure they will like it.<br /><br />3 stars. <br />This one didn't work for me.</span>

          </span>

In the end one has to be more important. Letting </b></span>

In the end one has to be more important. Letting go isn’t easy.<br><br>Blaire believed in her fairytale...<br> but no one can live in a fantasy.<br><br>Her love for Rush and desire to have a family keep her believing that they can find a way for this to work. Until she has to make the right decision for her and the baby. Even if it breaks her heart.<br><br>Can they find the forever that they both want or has it all just gone... too far?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398414ra/769981.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>So, Here we go......<br>TEASER 1:</b><br><br>"Grant and Nan have had a thing for a while now. Nan finally screwed things up for the last time and its over. Rush didn't know about it"<br><br>My mouth dropped open as Dean's words sank in. Grant and Nan? Really?<br><br>"Shocked the hell outta me too. Didn't think that boy was stupid. Guess he learned the hard way just cause it's pretty doesn't mean it shines"<br><br><br><b>BAD NEWS, PEOPLE!!!!</b><br><br><br><b>And, now TEASER 2:</b><br><br><i>The night breeze was cold now. I immediately shivered and Rush stopped and wrapped his arms around me. “We need to go to the house. I’m not going to make her stand out here and talk. It’s too damn cold.” Rush told his father.<br><br>Dean finally stopped walking and looked back at me. His eyes slowly took me in and I could see the moment he noticed my stomach.<br><br>“Dean, this is Blaire Wynn. My fiancée. Blaire this is Dean Finlay, my father.” Rush said in a tight voice. He didn’t sound like he wanted to make this introduction.<br><br>“No one told me I was gonna be a grandpa,” he said in a slow drawl. I wasn’t sure how he felt about that because there was no emotion on his face.<br><br>“I’ve been busy,” was the only response Rush gave him. That was odd. Was he embarrassed to tell his dad? I felt sick at my stomach and started to ease away from him.<br><br>His arms tightened their hold on me and I could feel his attention focused completely on me. “What’s wrong?” He asked turning his back on his father and bending down so he could look me directly in the eyes.<br><br>I didn’t want to have this conversation in front of Dean. I could feel his dad’s eyes on both of us. I shook my head but my body was still tense. I couldn’t help that. The fact he hadn’t told his father was bothering me.<br><br>“I’m taking her to the car. I’ll meet you back at the house,” Rush said over his shoulder but kept his eyes focused on mine. I dropped my gaze wishing I hadn’t reacted now. I was making a scene. Dean was going to think I was a whinny princess.</i><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380236618ra/681470.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>IS SHE FOR REAL??????</b><br><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409026ra/800604.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>"......'think' I was a whiny princess...."</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409026ra/800605.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Hahahaahahahahahaha.......(Sorry, had to get it out of my system)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/518394.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>But I don't care.....b'coz we are going to get more "RUSH" ladies.*woot woot*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409026ra/800606.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_637759122" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/637759122" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/637759122?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=july-reads">july-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer637759122" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15710958549195508255">This book was a fabulous ending to Rush and Blaire's romantic tale. It had everything that I love in a heart warming romance story. The sex was smoking hot, and Rush was his usual panty melting, dirty talking self. The only negative in the whole story was Nan; but I guess that is to be expected when it comes to her. There were some new characters thrown into the mix as well, so I am hoping that means we won't be seeing the last of the Rosemary bunch. We get to meet a character named: Captain; wh</span>
  <span id="freeText15710958549195508255" style="display:none">This book was a fabulous ending to Rush and Blaire's romantic tale. It had everything that I love in a heart warming romance story. The sex was smoking hot, and Rush was his usual panty melting, dirty talking self. The only negative in the whole story was Nan; but I guess that is to be expected when it comes to her. There were some new characters thrown into the mix as well, so I am hoping that means we won't be seeing the last of the Rosemary bunch. We get to meet a character named: Captain; who I will admit has me intrigued and crossing my fingers that he will get a story. As well as Nan's fathers daughter named: Harlow; she also has sparked my curiousity, and I think she would also make for a great story!! (Toes are crossed too!!) Not only did we have new characters, but we got to see all of our old ones that we have grown to know and love.<br /><br />Rush and Blaire are awaiting the birth of their child, but nothing can ever be 100% smooth sailing in romance land. Rush becomes aware that his sister Nan is in turmoil, and Blaire talks him in to taking her with him to help Nan out. When they show up, Rush is faced with the dillema of putting Nan before his beloved Blaire. He is once again torn, as in his heart he wants to be there for Blaire and only Blaire; but he also loves his sister and is terrified that she may hurt herself if he isn't there for her. This is a continuation of a problem that has happened between Rush and Blaire before. This time though, Blaire is pregnant and not willing to put up with some of the same old feelings that were experienced in the past. She leaves to go stay with her father, and ends up with a surprise of her own while she is there. I am relieved to state that Abbi Glines did not drag out the story line with Rush/Nan/and BLaire for too long. When I was reading this, I became concerned that the whole book was going to be about the conflict that arises with Nan. I am super glad to report that wasn't the case, as there was so many good things to focus on. We get to witness a beautiful wedding between Blaire and Rush, and I must say that I fell in love with Rush all over again through out the wedding preperations. He was so sweet in the gifts he got his fiance, I was extremely touched as I was reading it. All I have to say about that is two words: Pink, silk! You need to read it to find out; but trust me, it will have you tear up for sure.<br /><br />"Blaire, I love you girl..to the moon and back."--Rush Finlay<br /><br />Another touching scene is the birth of their child. Abbi Glines also wrote this beautifully, and so realistically I was in stitches for part of it. I am a mother myself, so to see how Blaire reacted in the birthing room was a riot! The added bonus is we get to see how their life is for a good month after the little one is born too!<br /><br />If you have followed Rush and Blaire's journey then this is a must read! I feel the fans got a real treat with this book, and it just reminds me of why I fell in love with this couple in the first place. Their love is pure and true, and I don't think I can ever get enough of this awesome couple. An all out feel good read that I enjoyed the whole way!<br /><br />"When you find your reason for living, hold onto it. Never let it go. Even if it means burning other bridges along the way."~Rush Finlay</span>
  <a data-text-id="15710958549195508255" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer3236543808915854546"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “When you find your reason for living, hold on to it. Never let it go. Even if it means burning other bridges along the way.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/>Rush:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409010i/800549.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Blaire:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409011i/800550._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409011i/800551.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I fell right back into the story as if I’d never put the books down. The writing was engaging, you could easily relate to the characters, the story kept you turning the pages, and there was that promised HEA.<br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> When you first looked at me<br/>I forgot to breathe <br/>that moment marked my hardened heart<br/>I vowed never to leave<br/>
</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/><i>Rush promised her fore</i></span>
  <span id="freeText3236543808915854546" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “When you find your reason for living, hold on to it. Never let it go. Even if it means burning other bridges along the way.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Rush:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409010i/800549.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Blaire:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409011i/800550._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409011i/800551.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I fell right back into the story as if I’d never put the books down. The writing was engaging, you could easily relate to the characters, the story kept you turning the pages, and there was that promised HEA.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> When you first looked at me<br>I forgot to breathe <br>that moment marked my hardened heart<br>I vowed never to leave<br>
</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><i>Rush promised her forever... but promises can be broken.<br>Torn between his love for his family and his love for Blaire, Rush has to find a way to save one without losing the other. In the end one has to be more important. Letting go isn’t easy.<br>Blaire believed in her fairytale... but no one can live in a fantasy.<br>Her love for Rush and desire to have a family keep her believing that they can find a way for this to work. Until she has to make the right decision for her and the baby. Even if it breaks her heart.<br>Can they find the forever that they both want or has it all just gone... too far?</i><br>My first reaction:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409011ra/800552.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Like, what else can you freaking put them through? <b>Never fear</b>, Abbi Glines got creative.<br>**Warning: rant ahead**<br><b>You’ve been warned…</b><br>Onto Nan. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409011ra/800553.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>You’d think, after everything that has happened she would <b>FINALLY</b> stop being a raging bitch…<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409011ra/800554.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/560382.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Shocking right? With all that <b>sparkling</b> personality we've seen, how could she not turn her life around?<br>She manipulates people<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409011ra/800555.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And doesn’t care about anybody but herself.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409011ra/800556.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I mean, holy hell Nan is psycho. I was so frustrated with her! I only have a few surviving strands of hair left on my head after all that hair pulling. <br>Blaire is a freaking angel sent down from heaven with the patience of a saint because one look at Nanette, te lo juro por dios, this would have been me:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409011ra/800557.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>*deep breaths* okay, I think I got it all out.<br><i>Moving on,</i> Rush was still as delectable as ever. Rush and Blaire have both come a long way since that first meeting at his house and you can just <b>feel</b> how strong their bond is. <br><i>
  <blockquote> “I’ll do whatever needs to be done to make her happy. But I’ll be the one making her happy. Always. Just me.” </blockquote>
</i><br>I never felt like they had things to resolve, and <i>Forever Too Far</i> really wasn't about that. It was more that everybody was getting in their way and they had to learn how to prioritize, especially Rush.<br> <i>
  <blockquote> “You’re afraid you and the baby won’t come first. You don’t want him to have to choose.” </blockquote>
</i><br>I also felt that <i>Forever Too Far</i> dealt a lot with family. It was about forgiving and opening up your heart once again and letting go of those who were holding you back. <br><i>
  <blockquote> Nothing in life was as precious as this woman. It never would be. I’d found my happiness.” </blockquote>
</i> <br>They had some rough times but it was nice to see them finally get their HEA. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “How far is too far?” I asked.<br>“It’s all too far. I want you right her beside me… forever.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer537186105" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6506756590358121718">Me reading this book: <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/336252.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>This series was a roller coaster. Book 1 was awesome. I couldn’t put it down and fell in love it immediately (except for the horrible cliff hanger ending). Book 2 was more middle of the road. Not as good as one and disappointing as a follow-up. But this book redeemed the series for me. It brought the ending up to a high note. <br/><br/>This book was a proper ending. I’ll still enjoy catching up with/seeing Rush and Blaire in Woods and Grant’s books, but now I won’t feel like their s</span>
  <span id="freeText6506756590358121718" style="display:none">Me reading this book: <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/336252.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This series was a roller coaster. Book 1 was awesome. I couldn’t put it down and fell in love it immediately (except for the horrible cliff hanger ending). Book 2 was more middle of the road. Not as good as one and disappointing as a follow-up. But this book redeemed the series for me. It brought the ending up to a high note. <br><br>This book was a proper ending. I’ll still enjoy catching up with/seeing Rush and Blaire in Woods and Grant’s books, but now I won’t feel like their story is unfinished. I loved everything about Rush and Blaire. Yes, Rush still had is idiot moments that caused me to want to<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/534658.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But it was only a couple times and he actually seemed to have his priorities straight in this book. Blaire’s one moment of stupidity wasn’t all that bad and I can’t even say it was really stupidity. She did what was best for her. Her only big mistake (in my opinion) was not leaving Rush a note or text. But I really didn’t blame her. She had to think of herself and her baby and the best thing for her was to leave the situation and the stress she was under. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I did love that we got to see their wedding, the song Rush wrote for her (and performed at their wedding), the birth of their son and we got to meet him (Nathan Rush Finlay aka Nate). All of that served as the perfect ending to their story. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I really enjoyed meeting Rush’s dad. After the disaster that has been their parents in this series, it was nice to finally like one of the parental units. Granted, he’s not the best dad in the world, but you could clearly see that he loves his son.<br><br>And since I’m on the topic of dads…I’ve now made my peace with Blaire’s dad. In the last book I felt like is apology was too quick and the whole story line was wrapped up too quickly with Blaire forgiving him too quickly. Maybe I just hold grudges (which I do) but I would have liked to see him really make an attempt to make it up to her as opposed to Blaire instantly forgiving him. But…things worked out well in this book.<br><br>Nan was just awful. Because this book wasn’t initially planned, Nan was an odd character. I didn’t like her quick turnaround in the second book and I didn’t trust it. And with this book she reverted back to her old self. And I hated her just as much as I did in the previous books. I wanted her to fall off a cliff and into the ocean. Or off the ends of the earth. I just wanted her to go away and never bother anyone ever again. She seriously left me wanting to <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/581588.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/534944.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/535014.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If I were Blaire and Rush, I would have been telling Nan: <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/581550.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There was one part of the Nan storyline that I was incredibly happy with. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I was glad to see that Nan and Grant are over. I can’t stomach the thought of a book about Nan. I know my inner vampire is showing but I was seriously hoping she wouldn’t make it out of her suicide attempt. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>I also really liked the addition of Harlow. I would love to see more of her and I really hope she gets a story.<br><br>I would definitely recommend this book to people. However, if you haven’t read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17333880.Twisted_Perfection__Perfection___1_" title="Twisted Perfection (Perfection, #1) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">Twisted Perfection</a>, I would avoid this until you do. The events of Twisted Perfection take place in the middle of this book (but you don’t see any of it, just one scene from Blaire’s POV) but there are a few details that bridge TP and its sequel. <br><br>This book is definitely worth reading and it’s a fitting ending to a story…the ending Rush and Blaire deserved.<br><br>My Rush: <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793698i/581597._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Rush and Blaire: <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409806i/802735._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="6506756590358121718" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('k5UfJ1WmwyKqWo+56me2aNcsjiZ9kjZPBJVZq3WE2uY5eQtHK2aquPu062yIz2ArEMdbImlMbJL2LLHkhXLOzw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer864978734716649100">Abbi Glines is a #1 New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of the Rosemary Beach, Sea Breeze, Vincent Boys, Field Party and Existence series. She never cooks unless baking during the Christmas holiday counts. She believes in ghosts and has a habit of asking people if their house is haunted before she goes in it. She drinks afternoon tea because she wants to be Britis</span>
  <span id="freeText864978734716649100" style="display:none">Abbi Glines is a #1 New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of the Rosemary Beach, Sea Breeze, Vincent Boys, Field Party and Existence series. She never cooks unless baking during the Christmas holiday counts. She believes in ghosts and has a habit of asking people if their house is haunted before she goes in it. She drinks afternoon tea because she wants to be British but alas she was born in Alabama. When asked how many books she has written she has to stop and count on her fingers. When she’s not locked away writing, she is reading, shopping (major shoe and purse addiction), sneaking off to the movies alone, and listening to the drama in her teenagers lives while making mental notes on the good stuff to use later. Don’t judge.<br /><br />You can connect with Abbi online in several different ways. She uses social media to procrastinate.<br /></span>
